              def testCommentLineWithLexeme

                  //HELLO
          
      321. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    321. 
            
            

            

                  123
          
      322. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    322. 
            
            

            

                HERE
          
      323.

            1

              def testBlockComment
